â”‚               let factor = Self::DECAY.powi(days as i32);                                                                                  â”‚

â”‚               self.capability = (self.capability * factor).max(Self::FLOOR);                                                               â”‚
â”‚               self.prestige = (self.prestige * factor).max(Self::FLOOR);                                                                   â”‚
